---
layout:   default
title:    "Speaker Travel Funds, Compensation, &amp; Mentorship for Tech Conference Talks"
---

<h1 class="s-title emojify">
Speaker Travel Funds, Compensation, &amp; Mentorship for Tech Conference Talks</h1><p class="s-description emojify">Marginalized people have less access to networks of conference organizers &amp; experienced speakers. People already in those networks can dismiss details as too obvious to mention — not realizing how many much of the system is invisible and unknowable from the outside . So we wind up systematically holding marginalized people at a disadvantage when competing against peers who have more privilege; better access to logistical support, morale support, and a mentors' expertise. It matters when we take steps to level the field for marginalized people to compete for speaking opportunities. Conferences benefit from having more candidates, more varied proposals, more opportunities to wow audiences with highly qualified speakers who bring something new to the table.</p><div Don't use passive voice, &amp; center on people. "Performance is rarely considered, but" -&gt; "You might consider performance only rarely, but"</div></div><div class="s-attribution"><div class="s-source s-twitter"><a href="https://twitter.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow"><div class="s-source-icon storifycon-source-twitter"></div></a></div><a href="http://twitter.com/sarahmei/status/682359560825262080" target="_blank" rel="nofollow" class="s-posted"><span data-timestamp="2015-12-31T00:36:11.000Z" class="timestamp">Thu, Dec 31 2015 00:36:11</span></a><div class="s-element-actions"><a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?in_reply_to=682359560825262080&amp;related=storify" target="_blank" title="Reply" class="twitter-newwindow twitter-reply">Reply</a><a href="http://twitter.com/intent/retweet?tweet_id=682359560825262080&amp;related=storify" target="_blank" title="Retweet" class="twitter-newwindow twitter-retweet">Retweet</a><a href="http://twitter.com/intent/favorite?tweet_id=682359560825262080&amp;related=storify" target="_blank" title="Favorite" class="twitter-newwindow twitter-favorite">Favorite</a></div><div class="s-clear"></div></div></div><div class="s-clear"></div></div></li><li data-eid="c9cd3d67c32c35264434dd73" data-type="quote" data-source="twitter" data-permalink="//twitter.com/sarahmei/status/682357765730246657" class="s-element s-element-quote"><div class="s-share-dropdown"></div><div class="s-element-container"><div class="s-quote s-element-content"><div class="s-quote-content"><div class="s-quote-avatar-author s-quote-avatar-twitter"><a href="http://twitter.com/sarahmei" target="_blank" class="s-quote-avatar"><img src="https://twitter.com/sarahmei/profile_image?size=bigger" alt="sarahmei"/></a><div class="s-quote-author"><a href="http://twitter.com/sarahmei" target="_blank" class="s-quote-author-name">Sarah Mei</a><a href="http://twitter.com/sarahmei" target="_blank" class="s-quote-author-username">@sarahmei</a></div></div><div class="s-quote-text emojify">2a. Never say "I". Your sentences should describe the attendee instead of the presenter. "You will learn" instead of "I will show."</div></div><div class="s-attribution"><div class="s-source s-twitter"><a href="https://twitter.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow"><div class="s-source-icon storifycon-source-twitter"></div></a></div><a href="http://twitter.com/sarahmei/status/682357765730246657" target="_blank" rel="nofollow" class="s-posted"><span data-timestamp="2015-12-31T00:29:03.000Z" class="timestamp">Thu, Dec 31 2015 00:29:03</span></a><div class="s-element-actions"><a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?in_reply_to=682357765730246657&amp;related=storify" target="_blank" title="Reply" class="twitter-newwindow twitter-reply">Reply</a><a href="http://twitter.com/intent/retweet?tweet_id=682357765730246657&amp;related=storify" target="_blank" title="Retweet" class="twitter-newwindow twitter-retweet">Retweet</a><a href="http://twitter.com/intent/favorite?tweet_id=682357765730246657&amp;related=storify" target="_blank" title="Favorite" class="twitter-newwindow twitter-favorite">Favorite</a></div><div class="s-clear"></div></div></div><div class="s-clear"></div></div></li><li data-eid="5d24eb3e96fce29235f056e4" data-type="quote" data-source="twitter" data-permalink="//twitter.com/sarahmei/status/682357215978586112" class="s-element s-element-quote"><div class="s-share-dropdown"></div><div class="s-element-container"><div class="s-quote s-element-content"><div class="s-quote-content"><div class="s-quote-avatar-author s-quote-avatar-twitter"><a href="http://twitter.com/sarahmei" target="_blank" class="s-quote-avatar"><img src="https://twitter.com/sarahmei/profile_image?size=bigger" alt="sarahmei"/></a><div class="s-quote-author"><a href="http://twitter.com/sarahmei" target="_blank" class="s-quote-author-name">Sarah Mei</a><a href="http://twitter.com/sarahmei" target="_blank" class="s-quote-author-username">@sarahmei</a></div></div><div class="s-quote-text emojify">2. Don't mention yourself. The proposal isn't about you.
